dismantle_t101 = {
 icon = generic_construction
 allowed = {}
 highlight_states = { state = 101}
 cost = 5
 fire_only_once = no
 days_remove = 60
 available = {num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 3}
 visible = {has_country_flag=reconstruct_6 controls_state = 101}
 modifier = {civilian_factory_use = 3}
 complete_effect = {
   101 = {
    set_building_level = {
      type = radar_station
      level = 0
      province = {
        all_provinces = yes
        level > 0
        }
      }
    }
   }
